class=\"et_pb_module et_pb_space et_pb_divider et_pb_divider_1 et-hide-mobile\">\n\t\t\t</div> <!-- .et_pb_column -->\n\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t</div> <!-- .et_pb_row --><div class=\" et_pb_row et_pb_row_8\">\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"et_pb_column et_pb_column_4_4  et_pb_column_14\">\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"et_pb_text et_pb_module et_pb_bg_layout_light et_pb_text_align_left  et_pb_text_8\">\n\t\t\t\t\n<h2 style=\"text-align: center;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 36pt;\">ABOUT INTRO MUSIC</span><br>\n</strong></h2>\n\n\t\t\t</div> <!-- .et_pb_text -->\n\t\t\t</div> <!-- .et_pb_column -->\n\t\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t</div> <!-- .et_pb_row --><div class=\" et_pb_row et_pb_row_9\">\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"et_pb_column et_pb_column_1_2  et_pb_column_15\">\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"et_pb_module et_pb_toggle et_pb_toggle_close  et_pb_toggle_0 et_pb_toggle_item\">\n\t\t\t\t<h5 class=\"et_pb_toggle_title\">What is an Intro?</h5>\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"et_pb_toggle_content clearfix\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\n<p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><strong>Intro is the short form of introduction – typically a short presentation or teaser.</strong> It intends to give a brief overview of a product, company, or a specific content to a potential audience.</p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"color: #ff0000;\"><em><strong>The action of introducing something to someone or to some audience</strong> </em></span></p>\n\n\t\t\t\t</div> <!-- .et_pb_toggle_content -->\n\t\t\t</div> <!-- .et_pb_toggle --><div class=\"et_pb_module et_pb_toggle et_pb_toggle_close  et_pb_toggle_1 et_pb_toggle_item\">\n\t\t\t\t<h5 class=\"et_pb_toggle_title\">Where do we find Intros?</h5>\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"et_pb_toggle_content clearfix\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\n<p style=\"text-align: justify;\">Intros can be found in connection with almost all media products such as books, movies, short videos, or music pieces. Companies use intros to start a product presentation or to present their business. To promote movies, trailers are most often used to introduce the main story in just a few minutes. It allows the audience to quickly find into the film, video or movie.</p>\n\n\t\t\t\t</div> <!-- .et_pb_toggle_content -->\n\t\t\t</div> <!-- .et_pb_toggle --><div class=\"et_pb_module et_pb_toggle et_pb_toggle_close  et_pb_toggle_2 et_pb_toggle_item\">\n\t\t\t\t<h5 class=\"et_pb_toggle_title\">What is so important about an Intro?</h5>\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"et_pb_toggle_content clearfix\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\n<p style=\"text-align: justify;\"><strong><em>To put it straight:</em></strong></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: center;\"><span style=\"color: #ff0000;\"><strong>An Intro has to captivate the audience instantly and entirely!</strong></span></p>\n<p style=\"text-align: justify;\">If this is not happening, most of your audience will move or click away within seconds. An Intro must also <strong>be honest</strong> and should <strong>reflect your content or story</strong>. So, as you can see, a perfect intro is of outstanding importance. No matter how amazing your actual content is, a cheap and boring intro will never warp enough people to watch your incredible content. Make sure they do – and <strong>create an awesome start for your media!</strong></p>\n\n\t\t\t\t</div> <!-- .et_pb_toggle_content -->\n\t\t\t</div> <!-- .et_pb_toggle --><div class=\"et_pb_module et_pb_toggle et_pb_toggle_close  et_pb_toggle_3 et_pb_toggle_item\">\n\t\t\t\t<h5 class=\"et_pb_toggle_title\">We Love to Create new Intro Designs!</h5>\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"et_pb_toggle_content clearfix\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\n<p style=\"text-align: justify;\">We are specialized in creating unique intros, teasers, trailers, and sound logos. We also provide short <strong>animations of a logo or product</strong>. Free-Intro-Music.com is one of the largest “ready to go” Royalty Free Intro Music libraries in the world. We create creative designs for <strong>businesses, products, cinematic trailers, logos, advertising products, industry products,</strong> and much more. If you need individual service, we love to get in touch, listen to your ideas and expectations and <strong>we advise you professionally and reliably</strong>.</p>\n\n\t\t\t\t</div> <!-- .et_pb_toggle_content -->\n\t\t\t</div> <!-- .et_pb_toggle -->\n\t\t\t</div> <!-- .et_pb_column --><div class=\"et_pb_column et_pb_column_1_2  et_pb_column_16\">\n\t\t\t\t\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"et_pb_module et_pb_toggle et_pb_toggle_close  et_pb_toggle_4 et_pb_toggle_item\">\n\t\t\t\t<h5 class=\"et_pb_toggle_title\">What is a Jingle?</h5>\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"et_pb_toggle_content clearfix\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\n<p style=\"text-align: justify;\">A Jingle is a short (usually a few seconds long) sound or audio piece. Jingles, or so called “hooks”, are usually closely associated with a TV series, commercial, a company, or brand. Basically every successful TV advertisement uses jingles, which most of us know for life.</p>\n\n\t\t\t\t</div> <!-- .et_pb_toggle_content -->\n\t\t\t</div> <!-- .et_pb_toggle --><div class=\"et_pb_module et_pb_toggle et_pb_toggle_close  et_pb_toggle_5 et_pb_toggle_item\">\n\t\t\t\t<h5 class=\"et_pb_toggle_title\">What is an Audio Logo?</h5>\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"et_pb_toggle_content clearfix\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\n<p style=\"text-align: justify;\">An Audio Logo or Sound Logo is usually a sound, tune or just a few arranged single tones which stand like a visual logo for a brand, company or a specific media composition. Remember the end of an Intel or the Coca Cola commercial</p>\n<h3 style=\"text-align: justify;\"><strong>So, what is the difference?</strong></h3>\n<p style=\"text-align: justify;\">There is no exact definition what the difference between a sound logo and a jingle actually is. Most people in the music industry use both terms synonymously and interchangeably. Maybe a good way to distinct both is to think of an Audio Logo as a short Jingle.</p>\n\n\t\t\t\t</div> <!-- .et_pb_toggle_content -->\n\t\t\t</div> <!-- .et_pb_toggle --><div class=\"et_pb_module et_pb_toggle et_pb_toggle_close  et_pb_toggle_6 et_pb_toggle_item\">\n\t\t\t\t<h5 class=\"et_pb_toggle_title\">Where do we find Jingles?</h5>\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"et_pb_toggle_content clearfix\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\n<p style=\"text-align: justify;\">A Jingle is typically used in commercials, for advertising or in TV series. Some of the most recognizable jingles are from the Universal Studios logo, 20 Century Pictures logo or Mc Donald’s. Remember the sounds of the Simpsons, Bonanza, Ghostbusters, or the Gummy bears most of use grew up with? You will likely never forget them.</p>\n\n\t\t\t\t</div> <!-- .et_pb_toggle_content -->\n\t\t\t</div> <!-- .et_pb_toggle --><div class=\"et_pb_module et_pb_toggle et_pb_toggle_close  et_pb_toggle_7 et_pb_toggle_item\">\n\t\t\t\t<h5 class=\"et_pb_toggle_title\">How is Lino Rise Media creating Jingles?</h5>\n\t\t\t\t<div class=\"et_pb_toggle_content clearfix\">\n\t\t\t\t\t\n<p style=\"text-align: justify;\">First of all, we dive into the customers brand or company. We need to picture our client’s products and outputs as close as we can to get an exact impression of what we are dealing with and to make sure we are all on the same page. After the acquisition process, we talk this through and try to match our client’s expectation. We kick off the design process and deliver some drafted ideas. This is followed by reviews, sound design, and motion design until the final product is delivered to our customer. We are specialized in every field to achieve an individual, professional, and suitable product for our clients all over the world.</p>\n\n\t\t\t\t</div> <!-- .et_pb_toggle_content -->\n\t\t\t</div>
